namespace = flavor_eth
country_event = {
	id = flavor_eth.1
	title = flavor_eth.1.t
	desc = flavor_eth.1.d
	picture = SHIP_SAILING_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = ETH
		NOT = {
			is_year = 1550
		}
		religion_group = christian
		any_owned_province = {
			has_discovered = POR
		}
		NOT = {
			war_with = POR
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 30
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		add_prestige = 5
		custom_tooltip = flavor_eth.1.a.desc
		set_country_flag = portuguese_embassy
		hidden_effect = {
			capital_scope = {
				POR = {
					discover_province = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		add_legitimacy = 5
		hidden_effect = {
			capital_scope = {
				POR = {
					discover_province = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.1.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		reverse_add_casus_belli = {
			target = POR
			type = cb_insult
			months = 60
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			capital_scope = {
				POR = {
					discover_province = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = flavor_eth.2
	title = flavor_eth.2.t
	desc = flavor_eth.2.d
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = ETH
		has_country_flag = portuguese_embassy
		NOT = {
			war_with = POR
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 7
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.2.a
		trigger = {
			is_neighbor_of = MAM
		}
		POR = {
			country_event = {
				id = flavor_eth.3
				days = 180
				tooltip = flavor_eth.2.3
			}
		}
		add_mil_power = 25
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.2.b
		add_adm_power = 50
		add_dip_power = 50
		add_mil_power = 50
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.2.c
		add_treasury = 150
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = flavor_eth.3
	title = flavor_eth.3.t
	desc = flavor_eth.3.d
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			ETH = {
				country_event = {
					id = flavor_eth.4
					days = 180
				}
			}
		}
		add_mil_power = -50
		add_papal_influence = 10
		reverse_add_opinion = {
			who = ETH
			modifier = opinion_military_aid
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.3.b
		add_prestige = -5
		hidden_effect = {
			ETH = {
				country_event = {
					id = flavor_eth.5
					days = 1825
				}
			}
		}
		reverse_add_opinion = {
			who = ETH
			modifier = opinion_refused_military_aid
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = flavor_eth.4
	title = flavor_eth.4.t
	desc = flavor_eth.4.d
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.4.a
		reverse_add_opinion = {
			who = POR
			modifier = opinion_military_aid
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = eth_mil_aid_from_portugal
			duration = 3650
		}
	}
}

		}

	}

	}

			factor = 90
		}

			name = eth_zara_yakob_centralisation
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.6.b

			factor = 10
		}
		Stab_Add50Percent = yes
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = flavor_eth.11
	title = flavor_eth.11.t
	desc = flavor_eth.11.d
	picture = ORTHODOX_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = ETH
		is_year = 1450
		NOT = {
			is_year = 1480
		}
		exists = MAM
		NOT = {
			vassal_of = MAM
			overlord_of = MAM
			alliance_with = MAM
			war_with = MAM
		}
		MAM = {
			religion_group = muslim
			owns = 358
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 7
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.11.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = oriental
			}
			add_opinion = {
				who = ETH
				modifier = opinion_good_relations
			}
		}
		MAM = {
			country_event = {
				id = flavor_eth.12
				days = 14
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.11.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_prestige = -10
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.11.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_casus_belli = {
			target = MAM
			type = cb_insult
			months = 1825
		}
		MAM = {
			country_event = {
				id = flavor_eth.13
				days = 14
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = flavor_eth.17
	title = flavor_eth.17.t
	desc = flavor_eth.17.d
	picture = ORTHODOX_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = MAM
		is_year = 1460
		exists = ETH
		religion_group = muslim
		ETH = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = eth_autonomous_church
			}
			religion = oriental
		}
		NOT = {
			vassal_of = ETH
			overlord_of = ETH
			alliance_with = ETH
			war_with = ETH
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 35
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.17.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		ETH = {
			add_opinion = {
				who = MAM
				modifier = opinion_irritated
			}
			country_event = {
				id = flavor_eth.18
				days = 14
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.17.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = flavor_eth.18
	title = flavor_eth.18.t
	desc = flavor_eth.18.d
	picture = ORTHODOX_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.18.a
		random_list = {
			30 = {}
			40 = {
				Stab_Subtract50Percent = yes
			}
			30 = {
				Stab_Subtract1 = yes
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			add_opinion = {
				who = MAM
				modifier = opinion_irritated
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = flavor_eth.19
	title = flavor_eth.19.t
	desc = flavor_eth.19.d
	picture = ORTHODOX_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = ETH
		religion = oriental
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 50
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					religion = oriental
					is_capital = no
				}
				set_province_flag = eth_strong_monastaries
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					religion = oriental
					is_capital = no
					not = {
						has_province_flag = eth_strong_monastaries
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = eth_strong_monastaries
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					religion = oriental
					is_capital = no
					not = {
						has_province_flag = eth_strong_monastaries
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = eth_strong_monastaries
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.19.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		random_list = {
			30 = {}
			40 = {
				Stab_Subtract50Percent = yes
			}
			30 = {
				Stab_Subtract1 = yes
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = eth_strong_monastaries
			}
			add_local_autonomy = -25
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.19.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		Stab_Add50Percent = yes
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = eth_strong_monastaries
			}
			add_local_autonomy = 25
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = flavor_eth.20
	title = flavor_eth.20.t
	desc = flavor_eth.20.d
	picture = ORTHODOX_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = ETH
		religion = oriental
		is_year = 1475
		NOT = {
			is_year = 1515
		}
		358 = {
			owner = {
				religion_group = muslim
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 4
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.20.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		Stab_Add50Percent = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.20.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		random_list = {
			30 = {}
			40 = {
				Stab_Subtract50Percent = yes
			}
			30 = {
				Stab_Subtract1 = yes
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = eth_independent_church
			duration = 3650
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = flavor_eth.26
	title = flavor_eth.26.t
	desc = flavor_eth.26.d
	picture = KING_SICK_IN_BED_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = ETH
		owns = 3009
		ruler_age = 40
		is_lesser_in_union = no
		has_heir = no
		government = monarchy
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 4
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.26.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		Stab_Add50Percent = yes
		define_heir = {
			claim = 100
			dynasty = ROOT
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = eth_mount_geshen
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.26.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		custom_tooltip = flavor_eth.26.b.tt
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = flavor_eth.27
	title = flavor_eth.27.t
	desc = flavor_eth.27.d
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		has_ruler = "Zara Yakob"
		NOT = {
			is_year = 1468
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = wih_eleniethiopia_flag
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 2
	}
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = wih_eleniethiopia_flag
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.27.a
		add_adm_power = 25
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_dlc = "Rights of Man"
				}
			}
			define_advisor = {
				type = statesman_NO
				name = "Eleni"
				culture = sidamo
				religion = oriental
				skill = 3
				female = yes
				discount = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Rights of Man"
			}
			define_consort = {
				name = "Eleni"
				country_of_origin = HDY
				dynasty = "Hadiya"
				culture = sidamo
				religion = oriental
				adm = 4
				dip = 4
				mil = 3
				female = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_queen_personality = righteous_personality
				add_queen_personality = intricate_web_weaver_personality
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = flavor_eth.28
	title = flavor_eth.28.t
	desc = flavor_eth.28.d
	picture = KING_SICK_IN_BED_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = ETH
		has_country_modifier = eth_mount_geshen
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 80
	}
	option = {
		name = flavor_eth.28.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		random_list = {
			30 = {}
			40 = {
				Stab_Subtract1 = yes
			}
			30 = {
				Stab_Subtract2 = yes
			}
		}
		remove_country_modifier = eth_mount_geshen
	}
}
